    var PREBID_USD_RATE = "0.7739";
    var PREBID_EUR_RATE = "0.65083";

        function calculatePfFromBidResponse(bidResponse) {
            var cpm = bidResponse.cpm * PREBID_EUR_RATE;
            var maxCpm = 80.00;

            if (cpm < 5.00) {
                return (Math.floor(cpm * 5) / 5).toFixed(2);
            } else if (cpm < 10.00) {
                return (Math.floor(cpm * 2) / 2).toFixed(2);
            } else if (cpm < 20.00) {
                return (Math.floor(cpm * 1) / 1).toFixed(2);
            } else if (cpm < maxCpm) {
                return (Math.floor(cpm * 0.2) / 0.2).toFixed(2);
            } else {
                return (maxCpm).toFixed(2);
            }
            return cpm;
        };

        function calculateCpmFromBidResponse(bidResponse) {
            var cpm = bidResponse.cpm;
            var maxCpm = 80.00;

            if (cpm < 10.00) {
                return (Math.floor(cpm * 100) / 100).toFixed(2);
            } else if (cpm < 40.00) {
                return (Math.floor(cpm * 5) / 5).toFixed(2);
            } else if (cpm < maxCpm) {
                return (Math.floor(cpm * 2) / 2).toFixed(2);
            } else {
                return (maxCpm).toFixed(2);
            }
            return cpm;
        };

        function getDemandFromBidResponse(bidResponse) {
            var demandSource = '';
            if (bidResponse && bidResponse.adId) {
                var demandPattern = /(adsrvr\.org)|(turn\.com)|(quantcast)|(mathtag)|(pr\.ybp\.yahoo\.com)|(doubleclick\.net)|(gwallet\.com)|(criteo)|(adnxs\.com)/i;
                try {
                    var demandFrom = demandPattern.exec(bidResponse.ad);
                    if (demandFrom) {
                        demandSource = demandFrom[0];
                    } else {
                        demandSource = 'other';
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    demandSource = 'error';
                }
            }
            return demandSource;
        };

        function getBidTimeFromBidResponse(bidResponse) {

            if (!bidResponse) return '';

            var bidTime = bidResponse.timeToRespond;
            var timeIncrement = 100;

            if (bidTime > 0)   {
                bidTime = Math.ceil(bidTime / timeIncrement) * timeIncrement;
            }

            return bidTime;
        };

                            } else if (adSize === '970x250' && adjustBidCpm < 12.00)  {
                                adjustBidCpm = 0;
                            } else if (adSize === '955x70' && adjustBidCpm < 3.50)  {
                                adjustBidCpm = 0;
                            } else if (adSize === '810x140' && adjustBidCpm < 6.50)  {
                                adjustBidCpm = 0;
                            }
                            return adjustBidCpm;
                        }
                    },pxyz: {
                        bidCpmAdjustment : function(bidCpm, bid){
                            // leaving (1) * (1) for currency and bid type readability
                            var adjustBidCpm = bidCpm * (1) * (1);
                            var adSize = bid.width + 'x' + bid.height;
                            if (adSize === '320x50' && adjustBidCpm < 5.00)  {
                                adjustBidCpm = 0;
                            } else if (adSize === '300x250' && adjustBidCpm < 5.00)  {
                                adjustBidCpm = 0;
                            }
                            return adjustBidCpm;
                        }
                    },ix: {
                        bidCpmAdjustment : function(bidCpm){
                            return bidCpm * (1/PREBID_USD_RATE) * (1);
                        }
                    },triplelift: {
                        bidCpmAdjustment : function(bidCpm){
                            return bidCpm * (1/PREBID_USD_RATE) * (1);
                        }
                    }
                };

                // Load the Prebid Javascript Library Async.
                loadScriptAsync("https://static.gumtree.com.au/master-867cc10a2aa8811570bb5d7515305c6ea31ca27d/_/prebid-min.js");

                for(var slotIx = 0; slotIx < adSlots.length; slotIx++)
                {
                    if(adSlots[slotIx].hasOwnProperty("biddable") && adSlots[slotIx].biddable) {

                        var slotPos = adSlots[slotIx].pos;

                        appnexusKvs.pos = slotPos;
                        rubiconInventory.pos = slotPos;

                        var pubmaticDctrSlot = pubmaticDctr.slice(0);

                        pubmaticDctrSlot.push("pos=" + slotPos);

                        var pubmaticDctrString = pubmaticDctrSlot.join("|");

                        //console.log(pubmaticDctrString);

                        var bids = [];
                        var bidCount = 0;

                        for(var prebidPartnerName in prebidPartnersConfig)
                        {
                            var partnerParamsBySize;
                            var pageSpecificPartnerParamsBySize;
                            if(typeof(pageSpecificPartnerParams) !== 'undefined') {
                                pageSpecificPartnerParamsBySize = pageSpecificPartnerParams[prebidPartnerName];
                            }
                            partnerParamsBySize = prebidPartnersConfig[prebidPartnerName];

                            var adSlotSizes = adSlots[slotIx].sizes;
                            var params = undefined;
                            for(var sx=0; sx< adSlotSizes.length; sx++) {
                                var adSlotSize = adSlotSizes[sx];
                                if(typeof(pageSpecificPartnerParamsBySize) !== 'undefined') {
                                    params = pageSpecificPartnerParamsBySize[JSON.stringify(adSlotSize)]; // Check if there is page specific params available
                                }
                                if(params == undefined) {
                                    params = partnerParamsBySize[JSON.stringify(adSlotSize)];
                                }
                                if(params !== undefined) {

                                    if (prebidPartnerName === "rubicon")   {
                                        params.inventory = rubiconInventory;
                                        params.visitor = rubiconVisitor;
                                    } else if (prebidPartnerName === "appnexus")   {
                                        for (var key in appnexusKvs) {
                                            if (appnexusKvs.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                                                params.keywords = params.keywords || {};
                                                params.keywords[key] = appnexusKvs[key];
                                            }
                                        }
                                    } else if (prebidPartnerName === "pubmatic")   {
                                        params.dctr = pubmaticDctrString;
                                    } else if (prebidPartnerName === "ix")   {
                                        try {
                                            if (params && params.sizeAsText) {
                                                params.size = JSON.parse(params.sizeAsText);
                                            }
                                        } catch (e) {
                                            console.log('GTAU:', e);
                                        }
                                    }

                                    var partnerBid = {};
                                    partnerBid.bidder = prebidPartnerName;
                                    partnerBid.params = params;

                                    bids[bidCount++] = partnerBid;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        if(bids.length > 0) {
                            window.adUnits.push(cloneObject({code: 'div-gpt-ad-632115744089839813-'+adSlots[slotIx].code, mediaTypes:{banner:{sizes: adSlots[slotIx].sizes}}, bids: bids}));
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (window.adUnits.length > 0) {
                    window.pbjs.que.push(function() {

                        window.pbjs.setConfig({ enableSendAllBids: true });
                        window.pbjs.setConfig({ bidderSequence: "random" });
                        window.pbjs.setConfig({ bidderTimeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT });

                        window.pbjs.setConfig({
                            userSync: {
                                filterSettings: {
                                    all: {
                                        bidders: '*',
                                        filter: 'include',
                                    },
                                },
                                syncsPerBidder: 1,
                                syncDelay: 7000,
                            }
                        });

                        // send KVs to Index
                        window.pbjs.setConfig( ixKvs );

                        window.pbjs.addAdUnits(window.adUnits);
                        window.pbjs.aliasBidder('appnexus', 'v_appnexus');
                        window.pbjs.aliasBidder('rubicon', 'v_rubicon');
                        window.pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();

                    });

                }

                function cloneObject(obj){
                    return (JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(obj)))
                }

                window.pbjs.que.push(function() {
                    window.pbjs.enableAnalytics({
                        provider: 'ga',
                        options: {
                            global: 'ga', // <string> name of GA global. Default is 'ga'
                            sampling: 0.05,
                            enableDistribution: false,
                            page: Gtau.Global.variables.dfpPage,
                            timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT,
                            screenSize: Gtau.Global.variables.screen.currentSize
                        }
                    });
                });
        }
    

    // asyn load google tag script
    loadScriptAsync(document.location.protocol + '//securepubads.g.doubleclick.net/tag/js/gpt.js');

    function filterHeaderStickyBannerSlot(gptadslots) {
        var allAdSlots = gptadslots,
            allAdSlotsLenght = allAdSlots.length,
            headerStickyBannerSlotName = 'leaderboard-header-large',
            bannerSlotName = '',
            i;

        for (i=0; i < allAdSlotsLenght; i+=1 ) {
            if (allAdSlots[i] && allAdSlots[i].o ) {
                bannerSlotName = allAdSlots[i].o.m || '';
                if ( bannerSlotName.indexOf(headerStickyBannerSlotName) >= 0 ) {
                    headerStickyBannerSlot.push(allAdSlots[i]);
                    allAdSlots.splice(i, 1);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    

    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        

        // disable initial load for the ad. It will be refreshed once each ad is rendered in DOM
        // we need this here on the top to be executed before rendering the slots
        googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();

        

        if (Gtau.Global.variables.gtmHeader.trackingViewModel) {
            var globalGTM = JSON.parse(Gtau.Global.variables.gtmHeader.trackingViewModel);
        }

        
            gptadslots[1] = googletag.defineSlot('/30720440/gumtree.web/home', [[970,250], [728,90], [1,1], [320,50], [320,120], [320,100]],'div-gpt-ad-632115744089839813-billboard')
                .defineSizeMapping(googletag.sizeMapping().
addSize([0, 0], []).

                .setTargeting('pos',['header'])

                .addService(googletag.pubads());
            //GTAU-21876 additional parameters via DFP

            gptadslots[2] = googletag.defineSlot('/30720440/gumtree.web/home', [[300,250]],'div-gpt-ad-632115744089839813-mrec-side')
                .defineSizeMapping(googletag.sizeMapping().
addSize([0, 0],[]).

            //GTAU-21876 additional parameters via DFP

            gptadslots[3] = googletag.defineSlot('/30720440/gumtree.web/home', [[320,50], [728,90]],'div-gpt-ad-632115744089839813-leaderboard-footer')
                .defineSizeMapping(googletag.sizeMapping().
addSize([0, 0], []).
addSize([340, 0], [320, 50]).
addSize([728, 0], [728, 90]).
addSize([1024, 0], []).
build())
                .setTargeting('pos',['bottom1'])
                .addService(googletag.pubads());
            //GTAU-21876 additional parameters via DFP
            gptadslots[3].setTargeting('analytics', [gptadslots[3].getTargeting('pos') +"|" + globalGTM.u.tg.mg]);
            
            gptadslots[4] = googletag.defineSlot('/30720440/gumtree.web/home', [[728,90]],'div-gpt-ad-632115744089839813-leaderboard-footer-desktop')
                .defineSizeMapping(googletag.sizeMapping().
addSize([0, 0], []).
addSize([1024, 0], [728, 90]).
build())
                .setTargeting('pos',['bottom1'])
                .addService(googletag.pubads());
            //GTAU-21876 additional parameters via DFP
            gptadslots[4].setTargeting('analytics', [gptadslots[4].getTargeting('pos') +"|" + globalGTM.u.tg.mg]);
            

        googletag.pubads().setTargetingWithUniqueKey = function(key, value) {
            var existingTargeting = this.getTargeting(key);
            var newTargeting = ((typeof existingTargeting) === 'string') ? [existingTargeting].concat(value) : existingTargeting.concat(value);
            return this.setTargeting(key, newTargeting);
        }


        
        googletag.pubads().setTargetingWithUniqueKey('pt',['Homepage']).setTargetingWithUniqueKey('li',['0']).setTargetingWithUniqueKey('hn',['gumtree.com.au']).setTargetingWithUniqueKey('g_hd',['a59QBGku1ZldobS+WSNIy+jP3mcVjWsUHHn9Wgzk0Hu/pN4qzE823abI8zfvYF2XmuW2Tn8T/mUBQ1Xr9uJWBg==']).setTargetingWithUniqueKey('hodor',['17']).setTargetingWithUniqueKey('ptg',['GTAU36697_A,GTAU31981_B,GTAU33199_A,GTAU35153_B,GTAU37115_A,GTAU38886_C,GTAU37829_B,GTAU34238_C,GTAU-37365_B']);
        googletag.pubads().setTargetingWithUniqueKey('test','prebid');
        
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('hb_lib_file', '/master-867cc10a2aa8811570bb5d7515305c6ea31ca27d/_/prebid-min.js');
        

        googletag.pubads().setTargetingWithUniqueKey('abtgroup','GROUP_10');

        

        var adtestUrl = new URL(window.location.href);
        var adtestKv = adtestUrl.searchParams.get("adtestkv");
        if (adtestKv) {
            adtestKv = adtestKv.replace(/\W/g, '');
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting('adtestkv', adtestKv);
        }

        
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('viewport', String(viewportWidth));

        if (typeof(viewportWidth) !== 'undefined') {

            var skinSize;

            if (viewportWidth >= 1550) {
                skinSize = ['li', 'lb'];
            } else if (viewportWidth >= 1440) {
                skinSize = 'lb';
            } else if (viewportWidth >= 700 && viewportWidth < 1440) {
                skinSize = 'm';
            } else if (viewportWidth >= 385 && viewportWidth < 700) {
                skinSize = 's';
            }

            if (skinSize) {
                googletag.pubads().setTargeting('skinsize', skinSize);
            }

        }

        //googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
        //googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering(); //by default
        googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
            var eventSlotId = event.slot && event.slot.getSlotElementId();

            if (event && !event.isEmpty) {
                var slotElement = eventSlotId,
                    bodyTypeBrowseElement;

                if (slotElement && slotElement.classList) {
                    slotElement.classList.remove('hidden-by-default-google-banner');
                }
                

            } else if(event && event.isEmpty && Gtau.Global.variables.googleConsoleEnabled) {
                console.group();
                console.warn('creativeSlotEmpty - ', event.isEmpty);
                console.warn('creativeSlotId - ', '#' + eventSlotId);

                console.log('adParentCategoryName - hg_garden');
                console.log('adCategoryName - hg_garden_lounging_relaxing');
                console.log('adCategoryId - 21016');
                console.log('adCssPageId - homenew');

                // changing console warn details as old details are not available anymore from the response
                console.warn('[Empty] creative for - ', event.slot.getSlotElementId());
                console.warn('event:', event);
                console.groupEnd();
            }
        });

        
        // disable loading banners if page is hidden and AB Testing 'isLoadBannersByPageVisibilitysEnabled'
        if (globalVariables.isLoadBannersByPageVisibilitysEnabled === 'true') {
            if ( widgets.pageVisibility && widgets.pageVisibility.isPageHidden() ) {
                googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
            }
        }
        googletag.enableServices();
    });

    // expose to window
    globalVariables.headerStickyBannerSlot = headerStickyBannerSlot;
    window.gptadslots = gptadslots;
    window.googletag = googletag;

    if(typeof(window.pbjs) !== 'undefined') {
        window.prebidTimeout = PREBID_TIMEOUT;
    }

}(window, window.jQuery, window.Gtau));

var googletag = googletag || {};

googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

function findObjectByKey(array, key, value) {
    for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
        if (array[i][key] === value) {
            return array[i];
        }
    }
    return null;
}

function gtag(options) {

    var slotElementId = 'div-gpt-ad-632115744089839813-' + options.adSlotId,
        hideUntilLoaded = (options.hideUntilLoaded === 'true'),
        adEl,
        AD_VICINITY_TO_SHOW = 500, // used to give a headstart request to the ad before the slot appeared in viewport
        SCROLL_THROTTLE_VALUE = 50; // used as a delay in ms. for the scroll event listener

    if (hideUntilLoaded) {
        adEl = document.getElementById(slotElementId);
        if (adEl && adEl.classList) adEl.classList.add('c-hide');
    }

    if (window.prebidAdSlots) {

        var slotfound = findObjectByKey(window.prebidAdSlots, 'code', options.adSlotId);

        if (!slotfound) {
            options.isPrebidEnabled = false;
        }
    }

    googletag.cmd.push(function() {

        var refreshed = false,
            adSlot,
            throttleTimeout,
            adEl = document.getElementById(slotElementId),
            definedAdHeight = parseInt(options.adHeight) || 0,
            // some ad slot has a css top style which causing confusion to get the actual top
            // below would try to get the number value of the css top style
            elementStyleTop = window.getComputedStyle(adEl).getPropertyValue('top').replace(/\D/g,'') || 0;


        // get the slot object from pubads by element id
        adSlot = googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(
            function(slot) {
                return slot.getSlotElementId() === slotElementId;
            }
        );

        /**
         * @name - isAdAlmostOrInViewport
         * @desc - method to check if the ad placeholder is almost visible to the user.
         */

        function isAdAlmostOrInViewport() {

            var adRect = adEl.getBoundingClientRect(),
                // if there's a css top style value > 0, it will place the blank ad slot to the middle,
                // that's why we need to set dividend to half of the pre-defined ad height
                dividend = (elementStyleTop > 0) ? 2 : 1,
                actualTop = definedAdHeight/dividend,
                viewportHeight = window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight;

            // only proceed when ad DOM element is present
            if (!adEl) return false;

            return (
                (adRect.bottom + (definedAdHeight/dividend) + AD_VICINITY_TO_SHOW) >= 0 &&
                adRect.top - actualTop <= viewportHeight + AD_VICINITY_TO_SHOW
            );
        }

        /**
         * @name - scrollHandler
         * @desc - method used to handle scroll event with throttle
         *         Note: defined a new one because can't make lodash throttle method to work with removeEvenListener
         *         Todo: try to look for a solution on how to use lodash throttle method
         */
        function scrollHandler () {
            if ( !throttleTimeout ) {
                throttleTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
                    throttleTimeout = null;
                    showAdHandler();
                }, SCROLL_THROTTLE_VALUE);
            }
        }

        /**
         * @name - preBidRequestBid
         * @desc - method to execute request bid for each ad slot
         */
        function preBidRequestBid() {

            window.pbjs.que.push(function () {
                if (window.dataLayer &&
                    window.dataLayer[0].u &&
                    window.dataLayer[0].u.mshue)
                {
                    window.pbjs.setConfig({
                        criteo: {
                            ceh: window.dataLayer[0].u.mshue
                        }
                    });
                }

                window.pbjs.requestBids({
                    adUnitCodes: [slotElementId],
                    timeout: window.PREBID_TIMEOUT,
                    bidsBackHandler: function (bidResponses) {

                        // pass to a variable every bid responses for logging/monitoring purposes

                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('g_prebid_version', window.pbjs.version);

                        if (bidResponses && slotElementId in bidResponses) {

                            window.prebidResponses = window.prebidResponses || {};
                            window.prebidResponses[slotElementId] = bidResponses[slotElementId];

                            window.pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync([slotElementId]);

                        }

                        if (adSlot) {
                            googletag.pubads().refresh(adSlot, {changeCorrelator: false});
                        }
                    }
                });
            });
        }

        /**
         * @name - showAd
         * @desc - method to show the ad whenever the placeholder is almost viewable to the user
         * @param - event
         */

        function showAdHandler () {
            if (!document.hidden && isAdAlmostOrInViewport() && !refreshed) {

                // variable to avoid multiple ad refreshes
                refreshed = true;

                if(window.adUnits && window.adUnits.length > 0) {
                    preBidRequestBid();
                } else {
                    // we still load it via dfp if prebid ad units if not available
                    if (adSlot) {
                        googletag.pubads().refresh(adSlot, {changeCorrelator: false});
                    }
                }

                // when ad has been displayed, clear all the event listener associated to that ad.
                window.removeEventListener('scroll', scrollHandler);
                document.removeEventListener('visibilitychange', showAdHandler);
            }
        }

        /**
         * @name - runLazyLoad
         * @desc - method to initialize event listeners for the lazy loading of the ad
         */
        function runLazyLoad() {

            if (isAdAlmostOrInViewport() && !refreshed) {
                showAdHandler();
            } else {

                // event listeners for ad refresh when it's in viewport.
                // scroll - actively check the ad whether it is already almost viewable to the user while scolling
                window.addEventListener('scroll', scrollHandler);

                // visibilitychange - so that if the user is coming from a different tab it will execute "showAd" method.
                document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', showAdHandler);
            }
        }

        // create the element placeholder for the ad
        // this should be always called before refresh
        googletag.display(slotElementId);

        if (options.isLazyLoadEnabled) {

            runLazyLoad();

        } else {

            if (options.isPrebidEnabled) {

                if(window.adUnits && window.adUnits.length > 0) {
                    preBidRequestBid();
                }
            } else {

                if (adSlot) {
                    googletag.pubads().refresh(adSlot, {changeCorrelator: false});
                }
            }
        }

        // reference: https://developers.google.com/doubleclick-gpt/reference?visit_id=0-636507205932962590-3426384474&hl=en&rd=1#googletageventsslotonloadevent
        googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotOnload', function(event) {
            if (event.slot && event.slot.getSlotElementId() !== slotElementId) return; // the event has fired, but for a different slot

            // only do it on a particular adslot, which is the billboard
            if (options.adSlotId === 'billboard') {
                jqCheck(function(){
                    reloadBxSlider($('[data-bxslider]'));
                });
            }

            // check if the jQuery is already loaded
            function jqCheck(fn) {
                var jqCheckCount = 0;
                var jqCheckInterval = setInterval(function(){
                    jqCheckCount += 1;
                    if (window.jQuery) {
                        clearInterval(jqCheckInterval);
                        if (typeof fn === 'function') {
                            fn();
                        }

                    }
                    // give up when reach maxium try - 3s
                    if (jqCheckCount === 6) {
                        clearInterval(jqCheckInterval);
                    }
                }, 500);
            }

            // check if the bxSlider is already loaded
            function reloadBxSlider($el) {
                if (jQuery.fn.bxSlider && $el.length && $el.data('gtauBxSlider')) {
                    $el.data('gtauBxSlider').reloadSlider();
                }
            }
        });

        googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {

            if (event.slot && event.slot.getSlotElementId() !== slotElementId) return; // the event has fired, but for a different slot

            if (event.size === null) {
                if (document.querySelectorAll('#' + slotElementId + ' iframe').length > 0) {
                    document.querySelectorAll('#' + slotElementId + ' iframe')[0].style.visibility = "hidden";
                }
            }

            // if the element was hidden, and an ad has been returned
            // although apparently the google lib will always show this div when the ad has loaded anyway
            if (options.hideUntilLoaded && !event.isEmpty) {
                var adEl = document.getElementById(slotElementId);
                if (adEl && adEl.classList) adEl.classList.remove('c-hide');
            }

        });

    });

}
  </script>

           <script type="text/javascript">
            function getSignInUrlWithRedirect(loginUrlPath) {
        var targetUrl = window.location.pathname;

        if(targetUrl === '/') {
            return window.location.href = loginUrlPath;
        }

        return window.location.href = loginUrlPath + '?targetUrl=' + encodeURIComponent(targetUrl);
    }
